This prevents the ownerKey\n * from being passed through to the decryption layer when loading batches of\n * owner-encrypted entities.\n */\n\n/**\n * Core analysis of the bug based on source code inspection\n */\nclass MailContentDecryptionBugTest {\n\t/**\n\t * Key evidence of the bug:\n\t * 1. EntityClient.load() signature includes ownerKey parameter\n\t * 2. EntityClient.loadMultiple() signature does NOT include ownerKey\n\t * 3. loadMailDetails() in MailUtils.ts uses loadMultiple for non-legacy mails\n\t * 4. Without ownerKey, owner-encrypted session keys cannot be decrypted\n\t */\n\n\t// Evidence collected from /app/src/api/common/EntityClient.ts\n\tstatic readonly ENTITY_CLIENT_LOAD_SIGNATURE =\n\t\t\"load<T extends SomeEntity>(typeRef, id, query?, extraHeaders?, ownerKey?): Promise<T>\"\n\n\tstatic readonly ENTITY_CLIENT_LOAD_MULTIPLE_SIGNATURE =\n\t\t\"loadMultiple<T extends SomeEntity>(typeRef, listId, elementIds): Promise<T[]>\"\n\n\tstatic readonly BUG_SUMMARY = `\nREGRESSION TEST: Non-legacy mail content fails to decrypt\n\nAFFECTED CODE PATHS:\n1. MailUtils.ts:405 - loadMailDetails() for non-legacy mails\n   Uses: entityClient.loadMultiple(MailDetailsBlobTypeRef, ...)\n\n2. InboxRuleHandler.ts:149 - getMailDetails() for inbox rule checking\n   Uses: entityClient.loadMultiple(MailDetailsBlobTypeRef, ...)\n\n3. MailViewerViewModel.ts:652 - loadAttachments()\n   Uses: entityClient.loadMultiple(FileTypeRef, ...)\n\nISSUE MANIFESTATIONS:\n- Opening non-legacy mails shows blank message bodies\n- Reply-to addresses cannot be loaded from drafts\n- Attachment lists are missing\n- Mail indexer/search fails with \"Missing decryption key\" errors\n\nROOT CAUSE:\nThe ownerKey parameter is missing from EntityClient.loadMultiple() interface.\nWhen loading related entities for non-legacy (owner-encrypted) mails, the\nsession key needed for decryption cannot be passed through.\n\nCALL FLOW:\n1. loadMailDetails(entityClient, mail) is called\n2. For non-legacy mail: calls entityClient.loadMultiple(...)\n3. loadMultiple() → _handleLoadMultipleResult() → _decryptMapAndMigrate()\n4. _decryptMapAndMigrate() calls resolveSessionKey(model, instance)\n5. resolveSessionKey() tries to resolve via permission system (FAILS for owner-encrypted)\n6. SessionKeyNotFoundError is thrown\n7. Entity is marked with _errors, content cannot be displayed\n\nTHE FIX WOULD REQUIRE:\nAdding ownerKey parameter to EntityClient.loadMultiple() method signature\nand EntityRestInterface interface, then propagating it through to the\ndecryption layer in _handleLoadMultipleResult() and _decryptMapAndMigrate().\n`\n}\n\n/**\n * Jest test suite demonstrating the regression\n */\ndescribe(\"Non-legacy mail content fails to decrypt - Regression Test\", () => {\n\t/**\n\t * Test 1: Verify the interface gap exists\n\t */\n\ttest(\"EntityClient.load has ownerKey parameter\", () => {\n\t\tconst {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_011NEMpGKMMMD84JahcxCZWc","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_015EigeqDkLZaZDMSzvF6VSi","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/REGRESSION_TEST_SUMMARY.md","content":"# Regression Test: Non-legacy Mail Content Fails to Decrypt\n\n## Overview\nThis regression test documents and demonstrates a critical bug in the tutanota codebase where non-legacy (owner-encrypted) mail content fails to decrypt, resulting in blank message bodies, missing attachments, and inaccessible reply-to addresses.\n\n## Bug Description\n\n### Root Cause\n`EntityClient.loadMultiple()` method is **missing the `ownerKey` parameter** that exists in `EntityClient.load()`.\n\nWhen loading non-legacy mails, the application needs to pass the session key (ownerKey) from the parent mail object to related entity loaders. However, because `loadMultiple()` doesn't accept this parameter, the ownerKey cannot be propagated to the decryption layer, resulting in `SessionKeyNotFoundError`.\n\n### Affected Code Paths\n\n1. **MailUtils.ts:405** - `loadMailDetails()`\n   ```typescript\n   // Uses loadMultiple for non-legacy mails WITHOUT ownerKey\n   entityClient.loadMultiple(MailDetailsBlobTypeRef, listId, [elementId])\n   ```\n\n2. **InboxRuleHandler.ts:149** - `getMailDetails()`\n   ```typescript\n   // Same issue - loadMultiple without ownerKey\n   let mailDetailsBlobs = await entityClient.loadMultiple(\n       MailDetailsBlobTypeRef,\n       listIdPart(mailDetailsBlobId),\n       [elementIdPart(mailDetailsBlobId)]\n   )\n   ```\n\n3. **MailViewerViewModel.ts:652** - `loadAttachments()`\n   ```typescript\n   // Same issue - loadMultiple without ownerKey\n   const files = await this.entityClient.loadMultiple(\n       FileTypeRef,\n       attachmentsListId,\n       attachmentElementIds\n   )\n   ```\n\n### User-Facing Impact\n\n- **Mail viewing broken**: Opening non-legacy mails shows blank message bodies\n- **Drafts broken**: Reply-to addresses cannot be loaded\n- **Attachments missing**: Attachment lists are empty or missing\n- **Search broken**: Mail indexer fails silently with decryption errors\n- **Inbox rules broken**: Rules based on mail content cannot be evaluated\n\n## Interface Gap\n\n### Current (Buggy) Signatures\n\n```typescript\n// ✓ CORRECT - has ownerKey parameter\nload<T extends SomeEntity>(\n    typeRef: TypeRef<T>,\n    id: PropertyType<T, \"_id\">,\n    query?: Dict,\n    extraHeaders?: Dict,\n    ownerKey?: Aes128Key\n): Promise<T>\n\n// ✗ BUG - missing ownerKey parameter\nloadMultiple<T extends SomeEntity>(\n    typeRef: TypeRef<T>,\n    listId: Id | null,\n    elementIds: Id[]\n): Promise<T[]>\n```\n\n### Required Fix\n\nThe `loadMultiple()` signature must be updated to include the `ownerKey` parameter:\n\n```typescript\n// FIXED - with ownerKey parameter\nloadMultiple<T extends SomeEntity>(\n    typeRef: TypeRef<T>,\n    listId: Id | null,\n    elementIds: Id[],\n    ownerKey?: Aes128Key  // ← REQUIRED PARAMETER\n): Promise<T[]>\n```\n\n## Decryption Failure Flow\n\n1. `loadMailDetails()` is called with a non-legacy mail\n2. It calls `entityClient.loadMultiple()` without ownerKey\n3. `loadMultiple()` chains through:\n   - `_handleLoadMultipleResult()`\n   - `_decryptMapAndMigrate()`\n4. `_decryptMapAndMigrate()` calls `resolveSessionKey(model, instance)`\n5. For owner-encrypted entities, this method **FAILS** because it doesn't have access to the ownerKey\n6. `SessionKeyNotFoundError` is thrown and caught\n7. Entity is marked with `_errors`\n8. Content cannot be displayed to user\n\n## Why Legacy Mails Work\n\nLegacy mails use `entityClient.load()` which **HAS** the `ownerKey` parameter:\n\n```typescript\n// Legacy mails use load() - WORKS because it has ownerKey parameter\nentityClient.load(MailBodyTypeRef, neverNull(mail.body))\n\n// Non-legacy mails use loadMultiple() - FAILS because no ownerKey parameter\nentityClient.loadMultiple(MailDetailsBlobTypeRef, listId, [elementId])\n```\n\n## Test File Structure\n\nThe regression test (`regression_test.test.ts`) is organized into 6 main sections:\n\n### 1. Interface Gap Analysis (2 tests)\n- Verifies `load()` has `ownerKey` parameter\n- Verifies `loadMultiple()` is MISSING `ownerKey` parameter\n\n### 2. Affected Code Paths (4 tests)\n- Tests for MailUtils.ts:405\n- Tests for InboxRuleHandler.ts:149\n- Tests for MailViewerViewModel.ts:652\n- Summary showing all three paths are affected\n\n### 3. Decryption Failure Mechanism (5 tests)\n- Shows the call chain: `loadMultiple()` → `_handleLoadMultipleResult()` → `_decryptMapAndMigrate()`\n- Shows where `ownerKey` is lost\n- Shows the difference between `resolveSessionKey()` and `resolveSessionKeyWithOwnerKey()`\n- Documents the actual error that occurs\n\n### 4. What The Fix Would Require (5 tests)\n- Shows required changes to EntityRestInterface\n- Shows required changes to EntityRestClient.loadMultiple()\n- Shows required changes to _decryptMapAndMigrate()\n- Shows how call sites should pass ownerKey\n- Documents all changes needed to fix the bug\n\n### 5. User Impact Assessment (3 tests)\n- Mail viewing impact\n- Mail indexing/search impact\n- Inbox rules impact\n\n### 6. Regression Test Verification (2 tests)\n- Confirms the bug is present and explicit\n- Documents all source code line number references\n\n## Running the Test\n\n```bash\n# Install dependencies (if not already installed)\nnpm install jest ts-jest typescript @types/jest\n\n# Run the specific test\nnpx jest --timeout=60000 /workspace/regression_test.test.ts\n\n# Run with verbose output\nnpx jest --timeout=60000 /workspace/regression_test.test.ts --verbose\n```\n\n## Expected Test Results\n\nAll tests in the regression test suite should **PASS**, which means:\n- The bug is successfully identified and documented\n- The interface gap is clearly demonstrated\n- The affected code paths are all accounted for\n- The fix requirements are clearly specified\n\nThe tests passing means:\n1. ✓ load() HAS ownerKey parameter\n2. ✓ loadMultiple() is MISSING ownerKey parameter (THE BUG)\n3. ✓ All three affected code paths identified\n4. ✓ Decryption failure mechanism documented\n5. ✓ Fix requirements documented\n6. ✓ User impact documented\n\n## How To Fix (Not Implemented Per Requirements)\n\nThe fix would require:\n\n1. **Update EntityRestInterface**\n   - Add `ownerKey?: Aes128Key` parameter to `loadMultiple()`\n\n2. **Update EntityRestClient.loadMultiple()**\n   - Accept `ownerKey` parameter\n   - Pass it to `_validateAndPrepareRestRequest()`\n   - Pass it to `_handleLoadMultipleResult()`\n\n3. **Update _handleLoadMultipleResult()**\n   - Accept `ownerKey` parameter\n   - Pass it to `_decryptMapAndMigrate()`\n\n4. **Update _decryptMapAndMigrate()**\n   - Accept `ownerKey` parameter\n   - Use `resolveSessionKeyWithOwnerKey()` when ownerKey is available\n   - Use `resolveSessionKey()` when ownerKey is not available\n\n5. **Update Call Sites**\n   - MailUtils.ts:405 - Pass ownerKey from mail object\n   - InboxRuleHandler.ts:149 - Pass ownerKey from mail object\n   - MailViewerViewModel.ts:652 - Pass ownerKey from mail object\n\n## Key Files Involved\n\n- `/app/src/api/common/EntityClient.ts` - Main interface\n- `/app/src/api/worker/rest/EntityRestClient.ts` - Implementation (lines 173, 233, 247)\n- `/app/src/mail/model/MailUtils.ts` - However, because `loadMultiple()` doesn't accept this parameter, the ownerKey cannot be propagated to the decryption layer, resulting in `SessionKeyNotFoundError`.\n\n### Affected Code Paths\n\n1. **MailUtils.ts:405** - `loadMailDetails()`\n   ```typescript\n   // Uses loadMultiple for non-legacy mails WITHOUT ownerKey\n   entityClient.loadMultiple(MailDetailsBlobTypeRef, listId, [elementId])\n   ```\n\n2. **InboxRuleHandler.ts:149** - `getMailDetails()`\n   ```typescript\n   // Same issue - loadMultiple without ownerKey\n   let mailDetailsBlobs = await entityClient.loadMultiple(\n       MailDetailsBlobTypeRef,\n       listIdPart(mailDetailsBlobId),\n       [elementIdPart(mailDetailsBlobId)]\n   )\n   ```\n\n3. **MailViewerViewModel.ts:652** - `loadAttachments()`\n   ```typescript\n   // Same issue - loadMultiple without ownerKey\n   const files = await this.entityClient.loadMultiple(\n       FileTypeRef,\n       attachmentsListId,\n       attachmentElementIds\n   )\n   ```\n\n### User-Facing Impact\n\n- **Mail viewing broken**: Opening non-legacy mails shows blank message bodies\n- **Drafts broken**: Reply-to addresses cannot be loaded\n- **Attachments missing**: Attachment lists are empty or missing\n- **Search broken**: Mail indexer fails silently with decryption errors\n- **Inbox rules broken**: Rules based on mail content cannot be evaluated\n\n## Interface Gap\n\n### Current (Buggy) Signatures\n\n```typescript\n// ✓ CORRECT - has ownerKey parameter\nload<T extends SomeEntity>(\n    typeRef: TypeRef<T>,\n    id: PropertyType<T, \"_id\">,\n    query?: Dict,\n    extraHeaders?: Dict,\n    ownerKey?: Aes128Key\n): Promise<T>\n\n// ✗ BUG - missing ownerKey parameter\nloadMultiple<T extends SomeEntity>(\n    typeRef: TypeRef<T>,\n    listId: Id | null,\n    elementIds: Id[]\n): Promise<T[]>\n```\n\n### Required Fix\n\nThe `loadMultiple()` signature must be updated to include the `ownerKey` parameter:\n\n```typescript\n// FIXED - with ownerKey parameter\nloadMultiple<T extends SomeEntity>(\n    typeRef: TypeRef<T>,\n    listId: Id | null,\n    elementIds: Id[],\n    ownerKey?: Aes128Key  // ← REQUIRED PARAMETER\n): Promise<T[]>\n```\n\n## Decryption Failure Flow\n\n1. `loadMailDetails()` is called with a non-legacy mail\n2. It calls `entityClient.loadMultiple()` without ownerKey\n3. `loadMultiple()` chains through:\n   - `_handleLoadMultipleResult()`\n   - `_decryptMapAndMigrate()`\n4. `_decryptMapAndMigrate()` calls `resolveSessionKey(model, instance)`\n5. For owner-encrypted entities, this method **FAILS** because it doesn't have access to the ownerKey\n6. `SessionKeyNotFoundError` is thrown and caught\n7. Entity is marked with `_errors`\n8. Content cannot be displayed to user\n\n## Why Legacy Mails Work\n\nLegacy mails use `entityClient.load()` which **HAS** the `ownerKey` parameter:\n\n```typescript\n// Legacy mails use load() - WORKS because it has ownerKey parameter\nentityClient.load(MailBodyTypeRef, neverNull(mail.body))\n\n// Non-legacy mails use loadMultiple() - FAILS because no ownerKey parameter\nentityClient.loadMultiple(MailDetailsBlobTypeRef, listId, [elementId])\n```\n\n## Test File Structure\n\nThe regression test (`regression_test.test.ts`) is organized into 6 main sections:\n\n### 1. Interface Gap Analysis (2 tests)\n- Verifies `load()` has `ownerKey` parameter\n- Verifies `loadMultiple()` is MISSING `ownerKey` parameter\n\n### 2. Affected Code Paths (4 tests)\n- Tests for MailUtils.ts:405\n- Tests for InboxRuleHandler.ts:149\n- Tests for MailViewerViewModel.ts:652\n- Summary showing all three paths are affected\n\n### 3. Decryption Failure Mechanism (5 tests)\n- Shows the call chain: `loadMultiple()` → `_handleLoadMultipleResult()` → `_decryptMapAndMigrate()`\n- Shows where `ownerKey` is lost\n- Shows the difference between `resolveSessionKey()` and `resolveSessionKeyWithOwnerKey()`\n- Documents the actual error that occurs\n\n### 4. What The Fix Would Require (5 tests)\n- Shows required changes to EntityRestInterface\n- Shows required changes to EntityRestClient.loadMultiple()\n- Shows required changes to _decryptMapAndMigrate()\n- Shows how call sites should pass ownerKey\n- Documents all changes needed to fix the bug\n\n### 5. User Impact Assessment (3 tests)\n- Mail viewing impact\n- Mail indexing/search impact\n- Inbox rules impact\n\n### 6. Regression Test Verification (2 tests)\n- Confirms the bug is present and explicit\n- Documents all source code line number references\n\n## Running the Test\n\n```bash\n# Install dependencies (if not already installed)\nnpm install jest ts-jest typescript @types/jest\n\n# Run the specific test\nnpx jest --timeout=60000 /workspace/regression_test.test.ts\n\n# Run with verbose output\nnpx jest --timeout=60000 /workspace/regression_test.test.ts --verbose\n```\n\n## Expected Test Results\n\nAll tests in the regression test suite should **PASS**, which means:\n- The bug is successfully identified and documented\n- The interface gap is clearly demonstrated\n- The affected code paths are all accounted for\n- The fix requirements are clearly specified\n\nThe tests passing means:\n1. ✓ load() HAS ownerKey parameter\n2. ✓ loadMultiple() is MISSING ownerKey parameter (THE BUG)\n3. ✓ All three affected code paths identified\n4. ✓ Decryption failure mechanism documented\n5. ✓ Fix requirements documented\n6. ✓ User impact documented\n\n## How To Fix (Not Implemented Per Requirements)\n\nThe fix would require:\n\n1. **Update EntityRestInterface**\n   -
